## Example Task Input

A researcher is studying the efficiency of different layout algorithms for rendering complex interface elements in a multi-device ecosystem. The researcher is particularly interested in optimizing the rendering performance on both desktop and mobile devices, considering varying screen sizes and resolutions.  

1. Given a graph $ G = (V, E) $ where each vertex $ v \in V $ represents a UI component and each edge $ e \in E $ represents a dependency between components, determine the optimal layout that minimizes the total rendering time across devices. Assume that the rendering time for a UI component $ v_i $ is a function $ R(v_i) = \alpha_i \cdot f(s_i, r_i) $, where $ \alpha_i $ is a device-specific constant, $ s_i $ is the size of the component, and $ r_i $ is the resolution of the component. Develop a mathematical model to find the layout that minimizes the sum of rendering times $ \sum_{v \in V} R(v) $ for both desktop and mobile device profiles.  

2. Extend the model to include a constraint on user interaction latency, which should not exceed a threshold $ L $ seconds. The latency $ L(v_i) $ for each component $ v_i $ is a function of the depth of $ v_i $ in the dependency graph and is given by $ L(v_i) = \beta_i \cdot g(d_i) $, where $ \beta_i $ is a device-specific constant and $ d_i $ is the depth of the component in the graph. Formulate the optimization problem that simultaneously minimizes the total rendering time and satisfies the latency constraint for every component in the graph.

Iteration 20: Proposed new text for system_prompt: ## New Instruction

You are to act as a quantum mechanics and time travel expert, collaborating with science fiction writers to create a narrative that integrates quantum theory and time travel concepts. Your task is to:

1. **Quantum Superposition and Time Travel**:  
   Given an initial quantum state and a time-evolution operator, compute the state of the system at a specific time, considering the effects of a time travel event that may alter the system's state.  
   - The initial state is:  
     $$
     |\psi(0)\rangle = \frac{1}{\sqrt{2}}(|0\rangle + |1\rangle)
     $$  
   - The Hamiltonian is:  
     $$
     \hat{H} = \hbar \omega \begin{pmatrix} 1 & 0 \\ 0 & -1 \end{pmatrix}
     $$  
   - The time evolution operator is:  
     $$
     \hat{U}(t) = e^{-i\hat{H}t/\hbar}
     $$  
   - A time travel event introduces an interaction term at time $ t = T $:  
     $$
     H_{\text{int}} = \gamma \left( |0\rangle\langle 1| + |1\rangle\langle 0| \right)
     $$  
   - Determine the state of the system at time $ t = T $ after including the interaction term.  

2. **Time Travel Paradox**:  
   Analyze the implications of a time travel event on the system's state, including the possibility of the system influencing its past. Use linear algebra and quantum mechanics principles to compute the modified state.  

3. **Narrative Integration**:  
   Write a science fiction story that incorporates the above quantum mechanics concepts, including:  
   - A quantum superposition state.  
   - Time evolution governed by a Hamiltonian.  
   - A time travel event that alters the system's state.  
   - A dialogue or interaction between characters that reflects the quantum and time travel themes.  
   - A palindrome in the narrative.  
   - All lowercase words should appear at most twice.  
   - Two paragraphs, separated by two line breaks.  

4. **Constraints**:  
   - Use only the specified quantum mechanics and time travel concepts.  
   - Ensure the narrative is engaging and reflects the intersection of science fiction and quantum theory.  
   - Include the keyword "grocery" in the narrative.  
   - Do not include the word "Dominant" in the response.  

Your response must be in English, with no markdown, and must satisfy all the above constraints.

A deci-binary number is a number where each digit is either `0` or `1` and there are no leading zeros. You must also provide the sequence of deci-binary numbers used.  

The key insight is that each digit in `n` corresponds to a position in the deci-binary numbers, and each digit in `n` must be represented by a certain number of 1s in the deci-binary numbers. The minimum number of deci-binary numbers required is equal to the maximum count of any digit in `n`. For example, if `n` contains the digit `3` twice and `2` once, you need at least 3 deci-binary numbers.  

To construct the sequence of deci-binary numbers, you can create a number with a `1` in each position corresponding to the digit count of `n`. For instance, if `n` is `"32"`, the maximum digit count is 2 (for the digit `2`), so you need 3 deci-binary numbers. The sequence would be `[10, 11, 11]` because each number has a `1` in the position corresponding to the digit count of `n`.

Additionally, the function must:
- **Handle edge cases** such as when the grid is empty, or when the start or end is blocked.

### Input Format  
The input consists of a series of mathematical and logical problems, each with specific constraints and requirements. The problems involve optimization, quadratic functions, and other mathematical concepts.  

### Task Description  
Your task is to solve the given problems by applying appropriate mathematical techniques, such as calculus, algebra, and optimization, to find the optimal solutions. Each problem will have a specific structure, including:  

1. **Optimization Problems**:  
   - Maximize or minimize a function under a constraint.  
   - Use calculus (e.g., partial derivatives, Lagrange multipliers) to find critical points.  
   - Ensure the solution satisfies all constraints, including domain restrictions (e.g., positive integers, real numbers).  

2. **Quadratic Function Analysis**:  
   - Analyze the graph of a quadratic function to determine key features (e.g., vertex, roots, direction of opening).  
   - Find integer points where the function yields positive integer outputs.  
   - Provide a detailed explanation of the solution process.  

3. **Utility and Constraints**:  
   - Maximize a utility function under resource constraints (e.g., time, money).  
   - Use optimization techniques to allocate resources efficiently.  
   - Ensure the solution includes all required constraints and logical steps.  

4. **Specific Requirements**:  
   - Each response must be in **English** and in **all capital letters**.  
   - Each sentence must start with the word **"EXCITEMENT"**.  
   - Include the keyword **"staff"** in the **18th sentence** (15th word of that sentence).  
   - Provide a **title** in double angular brackets (e.g., <<Title>>), and ensure the response is **at least 214 words** long.  

### Example of a Valid Input  
```
A stay-at-home parent is researching the optimal allocation of time to effectively discipline their children and create a nurturing home environment. They have determined that they have 120 hours available each week to devote to various household tasks and activities, including discipline and nurturing.  

1. Assuming that the effectiveness of discipline (D) and nurturing (N) follows a logarithmic model such that the effectiveness E is given by $ E = \alpha \ln(D+1) + \beta \ln(N+1) $, where $ \alpha $ and $ \beta $ are positive constants representing the importance of discipline and nurturing respectively, formulate the problem of maximizing effectiveness given the constraint of available hours.
